<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Announcing 18% increase to quarterly cash dividend </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill. &#150; July&nbsp;25, 2018 &#150; Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) today reported its second quarter 2018
results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We delivered a strong second quarter, in both developed and emerging markets, building on the momentum created in the
beginning of the year,&#148; said Dirk Van de Put, Chairman and CEO.&nbsp;&#147;We posted solid <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-line</FONT> results with good performance across all regions. We remain focused on executing against our plans and
will share the results of our strategic review with investors in September.&#148; </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><U>Second Quarter Commentary </U></I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net revenues</B> increased 2.1&nbsp;percent, including the impact of prior year divestitures. Organic Net
Revenue increased 3.5&nbsp;percent, which included the benefit of lapping the prior year&#146;s malware incident, and the negative impact of Easter shipment timing and the Brazil trucking strike. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross profit margin</B> was 41.6&nbsp;percent, an increase of 290 basis points driven primarily by a favorable
impact from currency and commodity hedging activities. Adjusted Gross Profit margin was 40.4&nbsp;percent, an increase of 60 basis points, driven by productivity savings and improved volume leverage. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating income margin</B> was 7.9&nbsp;percent, down 270 basis points, driven primarily by the impact from
pension participation changes in North America, partially offset by a favorable impact from currency and commodity hedging activities. Adjusted Operating Income margin increased 130 basis points to 16.7&nbsp;percent due to productivity savings and
lower selling, general&nbsp;&amp; administrative costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS</B> was $0.22, down 31&nbsp;percent, driven by the impact from pension participation changes in
North America and loss on debt extinguishment&nbsp;&amp; related expenses partially offset by a favorable impact from currency and commodity hedging activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EPS</B> was $0.56 and grew 15&nbsp;percent on a constant-currency basis, driven primarily by
operating gains. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Capital Return</B>: The company repurchased approximately $650&nbsp;million of its common stock and paid
approximately $300&nbsp;million in cash dividends. Year to date, the company has returned approximately $1.8&nbsp;billion. Today, the company&#146;s Board of Directors also declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.26 per share of Class&nbsp;A common
stock, an increase of 18&nbsp;percent. This dividend is payable on October&nbsp;12, 2018, to shareholders of record as of September&nbsp;28, 2018. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2018 Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International
provides guidance on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis, as the company cannot predict some elements that are included in reported GAAP results, including the impact of foreign exchange. Refer to the Outlook section in the
discussion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures below for more details. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company raised its full
year 2018 outlook for Organic Net Revenue growth to the high end of the previous range of 1 to 2&nbsp;percent. The company maintained its outlook for Adjusted Operating Income margin of approximately 17&nbsp;percent and double-digit Adjusted EPS
growth on a constant-currency basis. The company estimates currency translation would decrease net revenue growth by approximately 1 percent<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP> with no impact to Adjusted EPS<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>. In addition, the company continues to expect Free Cash Flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> of approximately $2.8&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z
International will host a conference call for investors with accompanying slides to review its results at 5 p.m. ET today. A listen-only webcast will be provided at <U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U>. An archive of the webcast will be available on
the company&#146;s web site. The company will be live tweeting the event at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Mondel&#275;z International </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (NASDAQ: MDLZ) is building the best snacking company in the world, with 2017 net revenues of approximately
$26&nbsp;billion. Creating more moments of joy in approximately 160 countries, Mondel&#275;z International is a world leader in biscuits, chocolate, gum, candy and powdered beverages, featuring global Power Brands such as <I>Oreo </I>and<I> belVita
</I>biscuits<I>; Cadbury Dairy Milk</I> and <I>Milka</I> chocolate; and <I>Trident</I> gum.&nbsp;Mondel&#275;z International is a proud member of the Standard and Poor&#146;s 500, NASDAQ 100 and Dow Jones Sustainability Index. Visit
<U>www.mondelezinternational.com</U> or follow the company on Twitter at <U>www.twitter.com/MDLZ</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>End Notes </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Organic Net Revenue, Adjusted Operating Income (and Adjusted Operating Income margin), Adjusted EPS, Adjusted
Gross Profit (and Adjusted Gross Profit margin), Free Cash Flow and presentation of amounts in constant currency are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures. Please see discussion of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures at the end of this press release for more information. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Additional Definitions </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Power Brands
include some of the company&#146;s largest global and regional brands, such as <I>Oreo</I>, <I>Chips Ahoy!</I>, <I>Ritz, TUC/Club Social</I> and <I>belVita</I> biscuits; <I>Cadbury Dairy Milk, Milka</I> and <I>Lacta</I> chocolate; <I>Trident</I>
gum; <I>Halls</I> candy; and <I>Tang</I> powdered beverages. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging markets consist of the Latin America region in its entirety; the
Asia, Middle East and Africa region excluding Australia, New Zealand and Japan; and the following countries from the Europe region: Russia, Ukraine, Turkey, Kazakhstan, Belarus, Georgia, Poland, Czech Republic, Slovak Republic, Hungary, Bulgaria,
Romania, the Baltics and the East Adriatic countries. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Developed markets include the entire North America region, the Europe region
excluding the countries included in the emerging markets definition, and Australia, New Zealand and Japan from the Asia, Middle East and Africa region.</P>

company&#146;s results of operations; the company&#146;s accounting for and the impact of U.S. tax reform; the company&#146;s liability related to partial withdrawal from the Bakery and Confectionery Union and Industry International Pension Fund and
timing of receipt of the assessment from the Fund; the impacts of the malware incident; the company&#146;s strategic review; and the company&#146;s outlook, including 2018 Organic Net Revenue growth, Adjusted Operating Income margin, Adjusted EPS
and Free Cash Flow. These forward-looking statements are subject to a number of risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond the company&#146;s control, which could cause the company&#146;s actual results to differ materially from those
indicated in the company&#146;s forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, risks from operating globally including in emerging markets; changes in currency exchange rates, controls and restrictions; continued
volatility of commodity and other input costs; weakness in economic conditions; weakness in consumer spending; pricing actions; tax matters including changes in tax rates and laws, disagreements with taxing authorities and imposition of new taxes;
use of information technology and third party service providers; unanticipated disruptions to the company&#146;s business, such as the malware incident, cyberattacks or other security breaches; competition; the restructuring program and the

<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:14pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. and Subsidiaries </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Reconciliation of GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>(Unaudited) </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company reports its
financial results in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;). However, management believes that also presenting certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
provides additional information to facilitate comparison of the company&#146;s historical operating results and trends in its underlying operating results, and provides additional transparency on how the company evaluates its business. Management
uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in making financial, operating and planning decisions and in evaluating the company&#146;s performance. The company also believes that presenting these measures allows
investors to view its performance using the same measures that the company uses in evaluating its financial and business performance and trends. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
company considers quantitative and qualitative factors in assessing whether to adjust for the impact of items that may be significant or that could affect an understanding of its ongoing financial and business performance and trends. The adjustments
generally fall within the following categories: acquisition&nbsp;&amp; divestiture activities, gains and losses on intangible asset sales and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairments, major program restructuring activities,
constant currency and related adjustments, major program financing and hedging activities and other major items affecting comparability of operating results. See below for a description of adjustments to the company&#146;s U.S. GAAP financial
measures included herein. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> information should be considered as supplemental in nature and is not meant to
be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with U.S. GAAP. In addition, the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may not be the same as or
comparable to similar <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures presented by other companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Because GAAP financial measures on a
forward-looking basis are not accessible and reconciling information is not available without unreasonable effort, the company has not provided that information with regard to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures
in the company&#146;s outlook. Refer to the Outlook section below for more details. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>DEFINITIONS OF THE COMPANY&#146;S <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and corresponding metrics reflect how the company evaluates its
operating results currently and provide improved comparability of operating results. As new events or circumstances arise, these definitions could change. When these definitions change, the company provides the updated definitions and presents the
related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> historical results on a comparable basis. When items no longer impact the company&#146;s current or future presentation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating results,
the company removes these items from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definitions. During the second quarter of 2018, the company added to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definitions the exclusion of the
impact from pension participation changes. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>&#147;Organic Net Revenue&#148; </B>is defined as net revenues excluding the impacts of acquisitions; divestitures; and currency rate fluctuations. The company also evaluates Organic Net Revenue growth from emerging
markets and its Power Brands. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>&#147;Adjusted Gross Profit&#148;</B> is defined as gross profit excluding the 2014-2018 Restructuring Program; acquisition integration costs; the operating results of divestitures; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative contracts; and incremental expenses related to the 2017 malware incident. The company also presents &#147;Adjusted Gross
Profit margin,&#148; which is subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Gross Profit. The company also evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted Gross Profit on a constant currency basis. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>&#147;Adjusted Operating Income&#148;</B> and <B>&#147;Adjusted Segment Operating Income&#148;</B> are defined as operating income (or segment operating income) excluding the impacts of the items listed in the
Adjusted Gross Profit definition as well as gains or losses (including <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impairment charges) on goodwill and intangible assets; divestiture or acquisition gains or losses and related divestiture,
acquisition and integration costs; impacts from resolution of tax matters; CEO transition remuneration; and impact from pension participation changes. The company also presents &#147;Adjusted Operating Income margin&#148; and &#147;Adjusted Segment
Operating Income margin&#148;, which are subject to the same adjustments as Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment Operating Income. The company also evaluates growth in the company&#146;s Adjusted Operating Income and Adjusted Segment
Operating Income on a constant currency basis. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>&#147;Adjusted EPS&#148;</B> is defined as diluted EPS attributable to Mondel&#275;z International from continuing operations excluding the impacts of the items listed in the Adjusted Operating Income definition as
well as losses on debt extinguishment and related expenses; gain on equity method investment transactions; net earnings from divestitures; gains or losses on interest rate swaps no longer designated as accounting cash flow hedges due to changed
financing and hedging plans; and U.S. tax reform discrete impacts. Similarly, within Adjusted EPS, the company&#146;s equity method investment net earnings exclude its proportionate share of its investees&#146; unusual or infrequent items. The tax
impact of each of the items excluded from the company&#146;s GAAP results was computed based on the facts and tax assumptions associated with each item and such impacts have also been excluded from Adjusted EPS. The company also evaluates growth in
the company&#146;s Adjusted EPS on a constant currency basis. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>&#147;Free Cash Flow&#148;</B> is defined as net cash provided by operating activities less capital expenditures. Free Cash Flow is the company&#146;s primary measure used to monitor its cash flow performance.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">See the attached schedules for supplemental financial data and corresponding reconciliations of the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures referred to above to the most comparable GAAP financial measures for the three months and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. See Items Impacting Comparability of Operating Results
below for more information about the items referenced in these definitions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SEGMENT OPERATING INCOME </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company uses segment operating income to evaluate segment performance and allocate resources. The company believes it is appropriate to disclose this
measure to help investors analyze segment performance and trends. Segment operating income excludes unrealized gains and losses on hedging activities (which are a component of cost of sales), general corporate expenses (which are a component of
selling, general and administrative expenses), amortization of intangibles, gains and losses on divestitures and acquisition-related costs (which are a component of selling, general and administrative expenses), in all periods presented. The company
excludes these items from segment operating income in order to provide better transparency of its segment operating results. Furthermore, the company centrally manages benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income and
interest and other expense, net. Accordingly, the company does not present these items by segment because they are excluded from the segment profitability measure that management reviews. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ITEMS IMPACTING COMPARABILITY OF OPERATING RESULTS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information is provided to give qualitative and quantitative information related to items impacting comparability of operating results. The company identifies these based on how management views the company&#146;s business; makes
financial, operating and planning decisions; and evaluates the company&#146;s ongoing performance. In addition, the company discloses the impact of changes in currency exchange rates on the company&#146;s financial results in order to reflect
results on a constant currency basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Divestitures, Divestiture-related costs and Gains/(losses) on divestitures </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Divestitures include completed sales of businesses and exits of major product lines upon completion of a sale or licensing agreement. Divestitures that
occurred in 2017 included the following: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

various licenses to use certain trademarks in connection with particular product categories in specified jurisdictions. On August&nbsp;17, 2017, the company entered into two agreements with KHC to terminate the licenses of certain <FONT

$247&nbsp;million Australian dollars ($187&nbsp;million as of July&nbsp;4, 2017) on the sale. The company also recorded divestiture-related costs of $2&nbsp;million and a foreign currency hedge loss of $3&nbsp;million during 2017. In the fourth

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Acquisitions and Acquisition-related costs </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&nbsp;7, 2018, the company acquired a U.S. premium biscuit company, Tate&#146;s Bake Shop, within its North America segment and extended its premium
biscuit offerings. On a constant currency basis, the purchase added incremental net revenues of $7&nbsp;million in the three months and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018.In addition, the company incurred acquisition-related costs of
$13&nbsp;million in the three months and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Acquisition integration costs </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within the company&#146;s AMEA segment, in connection with the acquisition of a biscuit operation in Vietnam in 2015, the company recorded integration costs of
$2&nbsp;million in the three months and $3&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 and $1&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>2014-2018 Restructuring Program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The primary
objective of the 2014-2018 Restructuring Program is to reduce the company&#146;s operating cost structure in both its supply chain and overhead costs. The program is intended primarily to cover severance as well as asset disposals and other
manufacturing-related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Restructuring costs </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded restructuring charges of $112&nbsp;million in the three months and $164&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 and
$148&nbsp;million in the three months and $305&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017 within asset impairment and exit costs or benefit plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-service</FONT> income. These charges were for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> asset write-downs (including accelerated depreciation and asset impairments), severance and other related costs. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Implementation costs </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Implementation costs primarily
relate to reorganizing the company&#146;s operations and facilities in connection with its supply chain reinvention program and other identified productivity and cost saving initiatives. The costs include incremental expenses related to the closure
of facilities, costs to terminate certain contracts and the simplification of the company&#146;s information systems. The company recorded implementation costs of $70&nbsp;million in the three months and $132&nbsp;million in the six months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2018 and $63&nbsp;million in the three months and $117&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Equity method
investee adjustments </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Within Adjusted EPS, the company&#146;s equity method investment net earnings exclude its proportionate share of its
investees&#146; unusual or infrequent items, such as acquisition and divestiture-related costs and restructuring program costs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and currency derivative contracts </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company excludes unrealized gains and losses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts) from
outstanding commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures until such time that the related exposures impact its operating results. The company recorded net
unrealized gains on commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivatives of $88&nbsp;million in the three months and $294&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018 and net unrealized losses of $46&nbsp;million in the three months
and $97&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Intangible assets gains and losses </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Impairment charges </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of 2017, the
company recorded a $38&nbsp;million intangible asset impairment charge resulting from a category decline and lower than expected product growth related to a gum trademark in its North America segment. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Incremental expenses related to the malware incident </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On June&nbsp;27, 2017, a global malware incident impacted the company&#146;s business. The malware affected a significant portion of the company&#146;s global
sales, distribution and financial networks. In the last four days of the second quarter and during the third quarter of 2017, the company executed business continuity and contingency plans to contain the impact, minimize damages and restore its
systems environment. To date, the company has not found, nor does the company expect to find, any instances of Company or personal data released externally. The company has also restored its main operating systems and processes and enhanced its
system security. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the second quarter of 2017, the company estimated that the malware incident had a negative impact of 2.3% on
its net revenue growth and 2.4% on its Organic Net Revenue growth. The company also incurred incremental expenses of $7&nbsp;million as a result of the incident. The company recognized the majority of delayed second quarter shipments in its third
quarter 2017 results, although the company permanently lost some revenue. On a 2017 full-year basis, the company estimated the loss of revenue had a negative impact of 0.4% on its net revenue and Organic Net Revenue growth. The company also incurred
total incremental expenses of $84&nbsp;million predominantly during the second half of 2017 as part of the recovery effort. The recovery from the incident was largely resolved by December&nbsp;31, 2017 and the company continued efforts to strengthen
its security measures and further mitigate cybersecurity risks. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Gain related to interest rate swaps </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recognized a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> loss of $5&nbsp;million in the three months and a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $9&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, within interest and other expense, net related to certain forward-starting interest rate swaps for which the planned timing of the
related forecasted debt was changed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Loss on debt extinguishment </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&nbsp;17, 2018, the company completed a cash tender offer and retired $570&nbsp;million of the long-term U.S. dollar debt. The company recorded a loss
on debt extinguishment of $140&nbsp;million within interest and other expense, net related to the amount the company paid to retire the debt in excess of its carrying value and from recognizing unamortized discounts, deferred financing and other
cash costs in earnings at the time of the debt extinguishment. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&nbsp;12, 2017, the company discharged $488&nbsp;million of its 6.500% U.S.
dollar-denominated debt. The company paid $504&nbsp;million, representing principal as well as past and future interest accruals from February 2017 through the August 2017 maturity date. The company recorded an $11&nbsp;million loss on debt
extinguishment within interest expense. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Impact from resolution of tax matters </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A tax indemnification matter related to our 2007 acquisition of the <I>LU</I> biscuit business was closed during the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. The
closure had no impact on net earnings, however, it did result in a $15&nbsp;million tax benefit that was fully offset by an $11&nbsp;million expense in selling, general and administrative expenses and a $4&nbsp;million expense in interest and other
expense, net. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of 2017, the Spanish Supreme Court decided, in the company&#146;s favor, an ongoing transfer pricing case with the
Spanish tax authorities related to businesses Cadbury divested prior to the company&#146;s acquisition of Cadbury. As a result of the final ruling, during the first quarter of 2017, the company recorded a favorable earnings impact of
$46&nbsp;million in selling, general and administrative expenses and $12&nbsp;million in interest and other expense, net, for a total <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> impact of $58&nbsp;million due to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> reversal of Cadbury-related accrued liabilities related to this matter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>CEO transition remuneration
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&nbsp;20, 2017, Dirk Van de Put succeeded Irene Rosenfeld as CEO of Mondel&#275;z International. In order to incent Mr.&nbsp;Van de Put
to join the company, the company provided him compensation to make him whole for incentive awards he forfeited or grants that were not made to him when he left his former employer. In connection with Irene Rosenfeld&#146;s retirement, the company
made her outstanding grants of performance share units for the 2016-2018 and 2017-2019 performance cycles eligible for continued vesting and paid $0.5&nbsp;million salary for her service as Chairman from January through March 2018. The company
refers to these elements of Mr.&nbsp;Van de Put&#146;s and Ms.&nbsp;Rosenfeld&#146;s compensation arrangements together as &#147;CEO transition remuneration.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company is excluding amounts it expenses as CEO transition remuneration from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results because those
amounts are not part of the company&#146;s regular compensation program and are incremental to amounts the company would have incurred as ongoing CEO compensation. The company incurred CEO transition remuneration of $10&nbsp;million in the three
months and $14&nbsp;million in the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>U.S. tax reform discrete impacts </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On December&nbsp;22, 2017, the United States enacted tax reform legislation that included a broad range of business tax provisions, including but not limited
to a reduction in the U.S. federal tax rate from 35% to 21% as well as provisions that limit or eliminate various deductions or credits. The legislation also causes U.S. allocated expenses (e.g. interest and general administrative expense) to be
taxed and imposes a new tax on U.S. cross-border payments, Furthermore, the legislation includes a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> transition tax on accumulated foreign earnings and profits. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain impacts of the new legislation would have generally required accounting to be completed in the period of enactment, however in response to the
complexities of this new legislation, the SEC issued guidance to provide companies with relief. The SEC provided up to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-year</FONT> window for companies to finalize the accounting for the impacts of this new
legislation and the company anticipates finalizing its accounting during 2018. While the company&#146;s accounting for the enactment of the new U.S. tax legislation is not complete, it has recorded an additional $2&nbsp;million discrete net tax
benefit, consisting of an $8&nbsp;million decrease in its transition tax liability that was partially offset by $6&nbsp;million of costs from other provisional tax reform updates. During the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2018, the company recorded
$87&nbsp;million in discrete net tax costs primarily comprised of an increase to its transition tax liability of $86&nbsp;million as a result of additional guidance issued by the Internal Revenue Service and various state taxing authorities, new
state legislation enacted during the period and further refinement of various components of the underlying calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Impact from pension
participation changes </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The impact from pension participation changes represent the charges incurred when employee groups are withdrawn from
multiemployer pension plans and other changes in employee group pension plan participation. The company excludes these charges from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results because those amounts do not reflect the company&#146;s
ongoing pension obligations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of 2018, the company implemented two aspects of its second revised last, best and final offer made
to the Bakery, Confectionery, Tobacco and Grain Millers Union with respect to 7 of 8 expired collective bargaining agreements. Implementation resulted in the company withdrawing from the Bakery and Confectionery Union and Industry International
Pension Fund (the &#147;Fund&#148;) with respect to those employees covered by the 7 collective bargaining agreements. In connection with that action, the company estimated a partial withdrawal liability of $567&nbsp;million and within its North
America segment, the company recorded a discounted liability and charge of $408&nbsp;million, $305&nbsp;million net of tax, which represents its best estimate of the partial withdrawal liability absent an assessment from the Fund. The company may
receive an assessment in 2018 or later, and the ultimate withdrawal liability may change from the currently estimated amount. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Constant currency
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management evaluates the operating performance of the company and its international subsidiaries on a constant currency basis. The company
determines its constant currency operating results by dividing or multiplying, as appropriate, the current period local currency operating results by the currency exchange rates used to translate the company&#146;s financial statements in the
comparable prior-year period to determine what the current period U.S. dollar operating results would have been if the currency exchange rate had not changed from the comparable prior-year period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>OUTLOOK </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company&#146;s outlook for 2018 Organic Net
Revenue growth, Adjusted Operating Income margin, Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis and Free Cash Flow are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude or otherwise adjust for items impacting
comparability of financial results such as the impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates, restructuring activities, acquisitions and divestitures. The company is not able to reconcile its full year 2018 projected Organic Net Revenue
growth to its full year 2018 projected reported net revenue growth because the company is unable to predict the impact of foreign exchange due to the unpredictability of future changes in foreign exchange rates, which could be material as a
significant portion of the company&#146;s operations are outside the U.S. The company is not able to reconcile its full year 2018 projected Adjusted Operating Income margin and Adjusted EPS growth on a constant currency basis to its full year 2018
projected reported operating income margin and reported diluted EPS growth because the company is unable to predict the timing of its Restructuring Program costs,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> impacts from commodity and forecasted currency transaction derivative contracts and impacts from potential acquisitions or divestitures well as the impact
of foreign exchange due to the unpredictability of future changes in foreign exchange rates, which could be material as a significant portion of the company&#146;s operations are outside the U.S. The company is not able to reconcile its full year
2018 projected Free Cash Flow to its full year 2018 projected net cash from operating activities because the company is unable to predict the timing and amount of capital expenditures impacting cash flow. Therefore, because of the uncertainty and
variability of the nature and amount of future adjustments, which could be significant, the company is unable to provide a reconciliation of these measures without unreasonable effort. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>
